<h2 dir=auto><a name=p-1511962-h-1 class=anchor href=#p-1511962-h-1></a>ÂÖàËµûÂêéÁúãÔºåÂÖªÊàê‰π†ÊÉØ</h2>
<p dir=auto>‰∏äÂõæÔºö<br>
WorkerÁΩëÈ°µ‰∏≠Ôºö<br>

<h2 dir=auto><a name=p-1511962-worker-4 class=anchor href=#p-1511962-worker-4></a>Â∞Ü‰∏ãÈù¢‰ª£Á†ÅÂ§çÂà∂Á≤òË¥¥Ëøõworker</h2>
<pre dir=auto class=codeblock-buttons><div class=codeblock-button-wrapper style=right:17px><button class="btn nohighlight copy-cmd" aria-label=Â∞Ü‰ª£Á†ÅÂ§çÂà∂Âà∞Ââ™Ë¥¥Êùø><svg class="fa d-icon d-icon-copy svg-icon svg-string" xmlns=http://www.w3.org/2000/svg><use href=#copy></use></svg></button><button class="btn nohighlight fullscreen-cmd" aria-label=ÂÖ®Â±èÊòæÁ§∫‰ª£Á†Å><svg class="fa d-icon d-icon-discourse-expand svg-icon svg-string" xmlns=http://www.w3.org/2000/svg><use href=#discourse-expand></use></svg></button></div><code class="hljs language-javascript" data-highlighted=yes><span class="hljs-title function_">addEventListener</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'fetch'</span>, <span class=hljs-function><span class=hljs-params>event</span> =&gt;</span> {
  event.<span class="hljs-title function_">respondWith</span>(<span class="hljs-title function_">handleRequest</span>(event.<span class=hljs-property>request</span>))
})

<span class="hljs-title function_">addEventListener</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'scheduled'</span>, <span class=hljs-function><span class=hljs-params>event</span> =&gt;</span> {
  event.<span class="hljs-title function_">waitUntil</span>(<span class="hljs-title function_">handleScheduled</span>(event.<span class=hljs-property>scheduledTime</span>))
})

<span class=hljs-keyword>async</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleRequest</span>(<span class=hljs-params>request</span>) {
  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> url = <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">URL</span>(request.<span class=hljs-property>url</span>)
  
  <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (url.<span class=hljs-property>pathname</span> === <span class=hljs-string>'/login'</span> &amp;&amp; request.<span class=hljs-property>method</span> === <span class=hljs-string>'POST'</span>) {
    <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> formData = <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> request.<span class="hljs-title function_">formData</span>()
    <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> password = formData.<span class="hljs-title function_">get</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'password'</span>)
    
    <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (password === <span class="hljs-variable constant_">PASSWORD</span>) {
      <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> response = <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Response</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>({ <span class=hljs-attr>success</span>: <span class=hljs-literal>true</span> }), {
        <span class=hljs-attr>headers</span>: { <span class=hljs-string>'Content-Type'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'application/json'</span> }
      })
      response.<span class=hljs-property>headers</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">set</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'Set-Cookie'</span>, <span class=hljs-string>`auth=<span class=hljs-subst>${PASSWORD}</span>; HttpOnly; Secure; SameSite=Strict; Path=/; Max-Age=86400`</span>)
      <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> response
    } <span class=hljs-keyword>else</span> {
      <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Response</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>({ <span class=hljs-attr>success</span>: <span class=hljs-literal>false</span> }), {
        <span class=hljs-attr>headers</span>: { <span class=hljs-string>'Content-Type'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'application/json'</span> }
      })
    }
  } <span class=hljs-keyword>else</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (url.<span class=hljs-property>pathname</span> === <span class=hljs-string>'/run'</span> &amp;&amp; request.<span class=hljs-property>method</span> === <span class=hljs-string>'POST'</span>) {
    <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (!<span class="hljs-title function_">isAuthenticated</span>(request)) {
      <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Response</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'Unauthorized'</span>, { <span class=hljs-attr>status</span>: <span class=hljs-number>401</span> })
    }
    
    <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleScheduled</span>(<span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Date</span>().<span class="hljs-title function_">toISOString</span>())
    <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> results = <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> <span class="hljs-variable constant_">CRON_RESULTS</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">get</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'lastResults'</span>, <span class=hljs-string>'json'</span>)
    <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Response</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>(results), {
      <span class=hljs-attr>headers</span>: { <span class=hljs-string>'Content-Type'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'application/json'</span> }
    })
  } <span class=hljs-keyword>else</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (url.<span class=hljs-property>pathname</span> === <span class=hljs-string>'/results'</span> &amp;&amp; request.<span class=hljs-property>method</span> === <span class=hljs-string>'GET'</span>) {
    <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (!<span class="hljs-title function_">isAuthenticated</span>(request)) {
      <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Response</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>({ <span class=hljs-attr>authenticated</span>: <span class=hljs-literal>false</span> }), {
        <span class=hljs-attr>headers</span>: { <span class=hljs-string>'Content-Type'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'application/json'</span> }
      })
    }
    <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> results = <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> <span class="hljs-variable constant_">CRON_RESULTS</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">get</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'lastResults'</span>, <span class=hljs-string>'json'</span>)
    <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Response</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>({ <span class=hljs-attr>authenticated</span>: <span class=hljs-literal>true</span>, <span class=hljs-attr>results</span>: results || [] }), {
      <span class=hljs-attr>headers</span>: { <span class=hljs-string>'Content-Type'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'application/json'</span> }
    })
  } <span class=hljs-keyword>else</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (url.<span class=hljs-property>pathname</span> === <span class=hljs-string>'/check-auth'</span> &amp;&amp; request.<span class=hljs-property>method</span> === <span class=hljs-string>'GET'</span>) {
    <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Response</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>({ <span class=hljs-attr>authenticated</span>: <span class="hljs-title function_">isAuthenticated</span>(request) }), {
      <span class=hljs-attr>headers</span>: { <span class=hljs-string>'Content-Type'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'application/json'</span> }
    })
  } <span class=hljs-keyword>else</span> {
    <span class=hljs-comment>// ÊòæÁ§∫ÁôªÂΩïÈ°µÈù¢ÊàñÁªìÊûúÈ°µÈù¢ÁöÑ HTML</span>
    <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Response</span>(<span class="hljs-title function_">getHtmlContent</span>(), {
      <span class=hljs-attr>headers</span>: { <span class=hljs-string>'Content-Type'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'text/html'</span> },
    })
  }
}

<span class=hljs-keyword>function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">isAuthenticated</span>(<span class=hljs-params>request</span>) {
  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> cookies = request.<span class=hljs-property>headers</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">get</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'Cookie'</span>)
  <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (cookies) {
    <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> authCookie = cookies.<span class="hljs-title function_">split</span>(<span class=hljs-string>';'</span>).<span class="hljs-title function_">find</span>(<span class=hljs-function><span class=hljs-params>c</span> =&gt;</span> c.<span class="hljs-title function_">trim</span>().<span class="hljs-title function_">startsWith</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'auth='</span>))
    <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (authCookie) {
      <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> authValue = authCookie.<span class="hljs-title function_">split</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'='</span>)[<span class=hljs-number>1</span>]
      <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> authValue === <span class="hljs-variable constant_">PASSWORD</span>
    }
  }
  <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> <span class=hljs-literal>false</span>
}

<span class=hljs-keyword>function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">getHtmlContent</span>(<span class=hljs-params></span>) {
  <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> <span class=hljs-string>`
  &lt;!DOCTYPE html&gt;
  &lt;html lang="en"&gt;
  &lt;head&gt;
    &lt;meta charset="UTF-8"&gt;

      button {
        background-color: #4CAF50;
        border: none;
        color: white;
        cursor: pointer;
      }
      #status {
        margin-top: 20px;
        font-weight: bold;
      }
      table {
        width: 100%;
        border-collapse: collapse;
        margin-top: 20px;
      }
      th, td {
        border: 1px solid #ddd;
        padding: 8px;
        text-align: left;
      }
      th {
        background-color: #f2f2f2;
      }
      #loginForm, #dashboard {
        display: none;
      }
    &lt;/style&gt;
  &lt;/head&gt;
  &lt;body&gt;
    &lt;div class="container"&gt;
      &lt;h1&gt;Worker Control Panel&lt;/h1&gt;
      &lt;div id="loginForm"&gt;
        &lt;input type="password" id="password" placeholder="Enter password"&gt;
        &lt;button onclick="login()"&gt;Login&lt;/button&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;div id="dashboard"&gt;
        &lt;button onclick="runScript()"&gt;Run Script&lt;/button&gt;
        &lt;div id="status"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
        &lt;table id="resultsTable"&gt;
          &lt;thead&gt;
            &lt;tr&gt;
              &lt;th&gt;Account&lt;/th&gt;
              &lt;th&gt;Type&lt;/th&gt;
              &lt;th&gt;Status&lt;/th&gt;
              &lt;th&gt;Message&lt;/th&gt;
              &lt;th&gt;Last Run&lt;/th&gt;
            &lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;/thead&gt;
          &lt;tbody&gt;&lt;/tbody&gt;
        &lt;/table&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;script&gt;
      let password = '';

      function showLoginForm() {
        document.getElementById('loginForm').style.display = 'block';
        document.getElementById('dashboard').style.display = 'none';
      }

      function showDashboard() {
        document.getElementById('loginForm').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('dashboard').style.display = 'block';
        fetchResults();
      }

      async function checkAuth() {
        const response = await fetch('/check-auth');
        const data = await response.json();
        if (data.authenticated) {
          showDashboard();
        } else {
          showLoginForm();
        }
      }

      async function login() {
        password = document.getElementById('password').value;
        const formData = new FormData();
        formData.append('password', password);
        const response = await fetch('/login', { 
          method: 'POST',
          body: formData
        });
        const result = await response.json();
        if (result.success) {
          showDashboard();
        } else {
          alert('Incorrect password');
        }
      }

      async function runScript() {
        const statusDiv = document.getElementById('status');
        statusDiv.textContent = 'Executing script...';
        try {
          const response = await fetch('/run', { method: 'POST' });
          if (response.ok) {
            const results = await response.json();
            displayResults(results);
            statusDiv.textContent = 'Script executed successfully!';
          } else if (response.status === 401) {
            statusDiv.textContent = 'Unauthorized. Please login again.';
            showLoginForm();
          } else {
            statusDiv.textContent = 'Error executing script.';
          }
        } catch (error) {
          statusDiv.textContent = 'Error: ' + error.message;
        }
      }

      async function fetchResults() {
        try {
          const response = await fetch('/results');
          if (response.ok) {
            const data = await response.json();
            if (data.authenticated) {
              displayResults(data.results);
            } else {
              showLoginForm();
            }
          } else {
            console.error('Failed to fetch results');
            showLoginForm();
          }
        } catch (error) {
          console.error('Error fetching results:', error);
          showLoginForm();
        }
      }

      function displayResults(results) {
        const tbody = document.querySelector('#resultsTable tbody');
        tbody.innerHTML = '';
        results.forEach(result =&gt; {
          result.cronResults.forEach((cronResult, index) =&gt; {
            const row = tbody.insertRow();
            if (index === 0) {
              row.insertCell(0).textContent = result.username;
              row.insertCell(1).textContent = result.type;
            } else {
              row.insertCell(0).textContent = '';
              row.insertCell(1).textContent = '';
            }
            row.insertCell(2).textContent = cronResult.success ? 'Success' : 'Failed';
            row.insertCell(3).textContent = cronResult.message;
            row.insertCell(4).textContent = new Date(result.lastRun).toLocaleString();
          });
        });
      }

      // È°µÈù¢Âä†ËΩΩÊó∂Ê£ÄÊü•ËÆ§ËØÅÁä∂ÊÄÅ
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', checkAuth);
    &lt;/script&gt;
  &lt;/body&gt;
  &lt;/html&gt;
  `</span>;
}

<span class=hljs-keyword>async</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleScheduled</span>(<span class=hljs-params>scheduledTime</span>) {
  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> accountsData = <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">parse</span>(<span class="hljs-variable constant_">ACCOUNTS_JSON</span>);
  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> accounts = accountsData.<span class=hljs-property>accounts</span>;
  
  <span class=hljs-keyword>let</span> results = [];
  <span class=hljs-keyword>for</span> (<span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> account <span class=hljs-keyword>of</span> accounts) {
    <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> result = <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">loginAccount</span>(account);
    results.<span class="hljs-title function_">push</span>(result);
    <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">delay</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">floor</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">random</span>() * <span class=hljs-number>8000</span>) + <span class=hljs-number>1000</span>);
  }

  <span class=hljs-comment>// ‰øùÂ≠òÁªìÊûúÂà∞ KV Â≠òÂÇ®</span>
  <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> <span class="hljs-variable constant_">CRON_RESULTS</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">put</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'lastResults'</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>(results));
}

<span class=hljs-keyword>function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">generateRandomUserAgent</span>(<span class=hljs-params></span>) {
  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> browsers = [<span class=hljs-string>'Chrome'</span>, <span class=hljs-string>'Firefox'</span>, <span class=hljs-string>'Safari'</span>, <span class=hljs-string>'Edge'</span>, <span class=hljs-string>'Opera'</span>];
  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> browser = browsers[<span class="hljs-title class_">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">floor</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">random</span>() * browsers.<span class=hljs-property>length</span>)];
  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> version = <span class="hljs-title class_">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">floor</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">random</span>() * <span class=hljs-number>100</span>) + <span class=hljs-number>1</span>;
  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> os = [<span class=hljs-string>'Windows NT 10.0'</span>, <span class=hljs-string>'Macintosh'</span>, <span class=hljs-string>'X11'</span>];
  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> selectedOS = os[<span class="hljs-title class_">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">floor</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">random</span>() * os.<span class=hljs-property>length</span>)];
  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> osVersion = selectedOS === <span class=hljs-string>'X11'</span> ? <span class=hljs-string>'Linux x86_64'</span> : selectedOS === <span class=hljs-string>'Macintosh'</span> ? <span class=hljs-string>'Intel Mac OS X 10_15_7'</span> : <span class=hljs-string>'Win64; x64'</span>;

  <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> <span class=hljs-string>`Mozilla/5.0 (<span class=hljs-subst>${selectedOS}</span>; <span class=hljs-subst>${osVersion}</span>) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) <span class=hljs-subst>${browser}</span>/<span class=hljs-subst>${version}</span>.0.0.0 Safari/537.36`</span>;
}

<span class=hljs-keyword>async</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">loginAccount</span>(<span class=hljs-params>account</span>) {
  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> { username, password, panelnum, type, cronCommands } = account
  <span class=hljs-keyword>let</span> baseUrl = type === <span class=hljs-string>'ct8'</span> 
    ? <span class=hljs-string>'https://panel.ct8.pl'</span> 
    : <span class=hljs-string>`https://panel<span class=hljs-subst>${panelnum}</span>.serv00.com`</span>
  <span class=hljs-keyword>let</span> loginUrl = <span class=hljs-string>`<span class=hljs-subst>${baseUrl}</span>/login/?next=/cron/`</span>

  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> userAgent = <span class="hljs-title function_">generateRandomUserAgent</span>();

  <span class=hljs-keyword>try</span> {
    <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> response = <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">fetch</span>(loginUrl, {
      <span class=hljs-attr>method</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'GET'</span>,
      <span class=hljs-attr>headers</span>: {
        <span class=hljs-string>'User-Agent'</span>: userAgent,
      },
    })

    <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> pageContent = <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> response.<span class="hljs-title function_">text</span>()
    <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> csrfMatch = pageContent.<span class="hljs-title function_">match</span>(<span class=hljs-regexp>/name="csrfmiddlewaretoken" value="([^"]*)"/</span>)
    <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> csrfToken = csrfMatch ? csrfMatch[<span class=hljs-number>1</span>] : <span class=hljs-literal>null</span>

    <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (!csrfToken) {
      <span class=hljs-keyword>throw</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Error</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'CSRF token not found'</span>)
    }

    <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> initialCookies = response.<span class=hljs-property>headers</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">get</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'set-cookie'</span>) || <span class=hljs-string>''</span>

    <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> formData = <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">URLSearchParams</span>({
      <span class=hljs-string>'username'</span>: username,
      <span class=hljs-string>'password'</span>: password,
      <span class=hljs-string>'csrfmiddlewaretoken'</span>: csrfToken,
      <span class=hljs-string>'next'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'/cron/'</span>
    })

    <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> loginResponse = <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">fetch</span>(loginUrl, {
      <span class=hljs-attr>method</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'POST'</span>,
      <span class=hljs-attr>headers</span>: {
        <span class=hljs-string>'Content-Type'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'</span>,
        <span class=hljs-string>'Referer'</span>: loginUrl,
        <span class=hljs-string>'User-Agent'</span>: userAgent,
        <span class=hljs-string>'Cookie'</span>: initialCookies,
      },
      <span class=hljs-attr>body</span>: formData.<span class="hljs-title function_">toString</span>(),
      <span class=hljs-attr>redirect</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'manual'</span>
    })

    <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (loginResponse.<span class=hljs-property>status</span> === <span class=hljs-number>302</span> &amp;&amp; loginResponse.<span class=hljs-property>headers</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">get</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'location'</span>) === <span class=hljs-string>'/cron/'</span>) {
      <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> loginCookies = loginResponse.<span class=hljs-property>headers</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">get</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'set-cookie'</span>) || <span class=hljs-string>''</span>
      <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> allCookies = <span class="hljs-title function_">combineCookies</span>(initialCookies, loginCookies)

      <span class=hljs-comment>// ËÆøÈóÆ cron ÂàóË°®È°µÈù¢</span>
      <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> cronListUrl = <span class=hljs-string>`<span class=hljs-subst>${baseUrl}</span>/cron/`</span>
      <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> cronListResponse = <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">fetch</span>(cronListUrl, {
        <span class=hljs-attr>headers</span>: {
          <span class=hljs-string>'Cookie'</span>: allCookies,
          <span class=hljs-string>'User-Agent'</span>: userAgent,
        }
      })
      <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> cronListContent = <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> cronListResponse.<span class="hljs-title function_">text</span>()

      <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class=hljs-string>`Cron list URL: <span class=hljs-subst>${cronListUrl}</span>`</span>)
      <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class=hljs-string>`Cron list response status: <span class=hljs-subst>${cronListResponse.status}</span>`</span>)
      <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class=hljs-string>`Cron list content (first 1000 chars): <span class=hljs-subst>${cronListContent.substring(<span class=hljs-number>0</span>, <span class=hljs-number>1000</span>)}</span>`</span>)

      <span class=hljs-keyword>let</span> cronResults = [];
      <span class=hljs-keyword>for</span> (<span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> cronCommand <span class=hljs-keyword>of</span> cronCommands) {
        <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (!cronListContent.<span class="hljs-title function_">includes</span>(cronCommand)) {
          <span class=hljs-comment>// ËÆøÈóÆÊ∑ªÂä† cron ‰ªªÂä°È°µÈù¢</span>
          <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> addCronUrl = <span class=hljs-string>`<span class=hljs-subst>${baseUrl}</span>/cron/add`</span>
          <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> addCronPageResponse = <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">fetch</span>(addCronUrl, {
            <span class=hljs-attr>headers</span>: {
              <span class=hljs-string>'Cookie'</span>: allCookies,
              <span class=hljs-string>'User-Agent'</span>: userAgent,
              <span class=hljs-string>'Referer'</span>: cronListUrl,
            }
          })
          <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> addCronPageContent = <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> addCronPageResponse.<span class="hljs-title function_">text</span>()

          <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class=hljs-string>`Add cron page URL: <span class=hljs-subst>${addCronUrl}</span>`</span>)
          <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class=hljs-string>`Add cron page response status: <span class=hljs-subst>${addCronPageResponse.status}</span>`</span>)
          <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class=hljs-string>`Add cron page content (first 1000 chars): <span class=hljs-subst>${addCronPageContent.substring(<span class=hljs-number>0</span>, <span class=hljs-number>1000</span>)}</span>`</span>)

          <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> newCsrfMatch = addCronPageContent.<span class="hljs-title function_">match</span>(<span class=hljs-regexp>/name="csrfmiddlewaretoken" value="([^"]*)"/</span>)
          <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> newCsrfToken = newCsrfMatch ? newCsrfMatch[<span class=hljs-number>1</span>] : <span class=hljs-literal>null</span>

          <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (!newCsrfToken) {
            <span class=hljs-keyword>throw</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Error</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'New CSRF token not found for adding cron task'</span>)
          }

          <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> formData = <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">URLSearchParams</span>({
            <span class=hljs-string>'csrfmiddlewaretoken'</span>: newCsrfToken,
            <span class=hljs-string>'spec'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'manual'</span>,
            <span class=hljs-string>'minute_time_interval'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'on'</span>,
            <span class=hljs-string>'minute'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'15'</span>,
            <span class=hljs-string>'hour_time_interval'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'each'</span>,
            <span class=hljs-string>'hour'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'*'</span>,
            <span class=hljs-string>'day_time_interval'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'each'</span>,
            <span class=hljs-string>'day'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'*'</span>,
            <span class=hljs-string>'month_time_interval'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'each'</span>,
            <span class=hljs-string>'month'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'*'</span>,
            <span class=hljs-string>'dow_time_interval'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'each'</span>,
            <span class=hljs-string>'dow'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'*'</span>,
            <span class=hljs-string>'command'</span>: cronCommand,
            <span class=hljs-string>'comment'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'Auto added cron job'</span>
          })

          <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'Form data being sent:'</span>, formData.<span class="hljs-title function_">toString</span>())

          <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> { success, <span class=hljs-attr>response</span>: addCronResponse, <span class=hljs-attr>content</span>: addCronResponseContent } = <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">addCronWithRetry</span>(addCronUrl, {
            <span class=hljs-attr>method</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'POST'</span>,

              <span class=hljs-string>'User-Agent'</span>: userAgent,
              <span class=hljs-string>'Referer'</span>: addCronUrl,
              <span class=hljs-string>'Origin'</span>: baseUrl,
              <span class=hljs-string>'Accept'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8'</span>,

              <span class=hljs-string>'Upgrade-Insecure-Requests'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'1'</span>
            },
            <span class=hljs-attr>body</span>: formData.<span class="hljs-title function_">toString</span>(),
          })

          <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'Full response content:'</span>, addCronResponseContent)

          <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (success) {
            <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (addCronResponseContent.<span class="hljs-title function_">includes</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'Cron job has been added'</span>) || addCronResponseContent.<span class="hljs-title function_">includes</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'Zadanie cron zosta≈Ço dodane'</span>)) {
              <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> message = <span class=hljs-string>`Ê∑ªÂä†‰∫ÜÊñ∞ÁöÑ cron ‰ªªÂä°Ôºö<span class=hljs-subst>${cronCommand}</span>`</span>;
              <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(message);
              <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">sendTelegramMessage</span>(<span class=hljs-string>`Ë¥¶Âè∑ <span class=hljs-subst>${username}</span> (<span class=hljs-subst>${type}</span>) <span class=hljs-subst>${message}</span>`</span>);
              cronResults.<span class="hljs-title function_">push</span>({ <span class=hljs-attr>success</span>: <span class=hljs-literal>true</span>, message });
            } <span class=hljs-keyword>else</span> {
              <span class=hljs-comment>// Â¶ÇÊûúÂìçÂ∫î‰∏≠Ê≤°ÊúâÊàêÂäü‰ø°ÊÅØÔºåÂÜçÊ¨°Ê£ÄÊü•cronÂàóË°®</span>

                }
              });
              <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> checkCronListContent = <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> checkCronListResponse.<span class="hljs-title function_">text</span>();
              
              <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (checkCronListContent.<span class="hljs-title function_">includes</span>(cronCommand)) {
                <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> message = <span class=hljs-string>`Á°ÆËÆ§Ê∑ªÂä†‰∫ÜÊñ∞ÁöÑ cron ‰ªªÂä°Ôºö<span class=hljs-subst>${cronCommand}</span>`</span>;

                cronResults.<span class="hljs-title function_">push</span>({ <span class=hljs-attr>success</span>: <span class=hljs-literal>true</span>, message });
              } <span class=hljs-keyword>else</span> {
                <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> message = <span class=hljs-string>`Â∞ùËØïÊ∑ªÂä† cron ‰ªªÂä°Ôºö<span class=hljs-subst>${cronCommand}</span>Ôºå‰ΩÜÂú®ÂàóË°®‰∏≠Êú™ÊâæÂà∞„ÄÇÂèØËÉΩÊ∑ªÂä†Â§±Ë¥•„ÄÇ`</span>;
                <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">error</span>(message);
                cronResults.<span class="hljs-title function_">push</span>({ <span class=hljs-attr>success</span>: <span class=hljs-literal>false</span>, message });
              }
            }
          } <span class=hljs-keyword>else</span> {
            <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> message = <span class=hljs-string>`Ê∑ªÂä† cron ‰ªªÂä°Â§±Ë¥•Ôºö<span class=hljs-subst>${cronCommand}</span>`</span>;
            <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">error</span>(message);
            cronResults.<span class="hljs-title function_">push</span>({ <span class=hljs-attr>success</span>: <span class=hljs-literal>false</span>, message });
          }
        } <span class=hljs-keyword>else</span> {
          <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> message = <span class=hljs-string>`cron ‰ªªÂä°Â∑≤Â≠òÂú®Ôºö<span class=hljs-subst>${cronCommand}</span>`</span>;
          <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(message);
          cronResults.<span class="hljs-title function_">push</span>({ <span class=hljs-attr>success</span>: <span class=hljs-literal>true</span>, message });
        }
      }
      <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> { username, type, cronResults, <span class=hljs-attr>lastRun</span>: <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Date</span>().<span class="hljs-title function_">toISOString</span>() };
    } <span class=hljs-keyword>else</span> {
      <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> message = <span class=hljs-string>`ÁôªÂΩïÂ§±Ë¥•ÔºåÊú™Áü•ÂéüÂõ†„ÄÇËØ∑Ê£ÄÊü•Ë¥¶Âè∑ÂíåÂØÜÁ†ÅÊòØÂê¶Ê≠£Á°Æ„ÄÇ`</span>;
      <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">error</span>(message);
      <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> { username, type, <span class=hljs-attr>cronResults</span>: [{ <span class=hljs-attr>success</span>: <span class=hljs-literal>false</span>, message }], <span class=hljs-attr>lastRun</span>: <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Date</span>().<span class="hljs-title function_">toISOString</span>() };
    }
  } <span class=hljs-keyword>catch</span> (error) {
    <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> message = <span class=hljs-string>`ÁôªÂΩïÊàñÊ∑ªÂä† cron ‰ªªÂä°Êó∂Âá∫Áé∞ÈîôËØØ: <span class=hljs-subst>${error.message}</span>`</span>;
    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">error</span>(message);
    <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> { username, type, <span class=hljs-attr>cronResults</span>: [{ <span class=hljs-attr>success</span>: <span class=hljs-literal>false</span>, message }], <span class=hljs-attr>lastRun</span>: <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Date</span>().<span class="hljs-title function_">toISOString</span>() };
  }
}

<span class=hljs-keyword>async</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">addCronWithRetry</span>(<span class=hljs-params>url, options, maxRetries = <span class=hljs-number>3</span></span>) {
  <span class=hljs-keyword>for</span> (<span class=hljs-keyword>let</span> i = <span class=hljs-number>0</span>; i &lt; maxRetries; i++) {
    <span class=hljs-keyword>try</span> {
      <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> response = <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">fetch</span>(url, options);
      <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> responseContent = <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> response.<span class="hljs-title function_">text</span>();
      <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class=hljs-string>`Attempt <span class=hljs-subst>${i + <span class=hljs-number>1</span>}</span> response status:`</span>, response.<span class=hljs-property>status</span>);
      <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class=hljs-string>`Attempt <span class=hljs-subst>${i + <span class=hljs-number>1</span>}</span> response content (first 1000 chars):`</span>, responseContent.<span class="hljs-title function_">substring</span>(<span class=hljs-number>0</span>, <span class=hljs-number>1000</span>));
      
      <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (response.<span class=hljs-property>status</span> === <span class=hljs-number>200</span> || response.<span class=hljs-property>status</span> === <span class=hljs-number>302</span> || responseContent.<span class="hljs-title function_">includes</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'Cron job has been added'</span>) || responseContent.<span class="hljs-title function_">includes</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'Zadanie cron zosta≈Ço dodane'</span>)) {
        <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> { <span class=hljs-attr>success</span>: <span class=hljs-literal>true</span>, response, <span class=hljs-attr>content</span>: responseContent };
      }
    } <span class=hljs-keyword>catch</span> (error) {
      <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">error</span>(<span class=hljs-string>`Attempt <span class=hljs-subst>${i + <span class=hljs-number>1</span>}</span> failed:`</span>, error);
    }
    <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">delay</span>(<span class=hljs-number>2000</span>); <span class=hljs-comment>// Wait 2 seconds before retrying</span>
  }
  <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> { <span class=hljs-attr>success</span>: <span class=hljs-literal>false</span> };
}

<span class=hljs-keyword>function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">combineCookies</span>(<span class=hljs-params>cookies1, cookies2</span>) {
  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> cookieMap = <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Map</span>()
  
  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">parseCookies</span> = (<span class=hljs-params>cookieString</span>) =&gt; {
    cookieString.<span class="hljs-title function_">split</span>(<span class=hljs-string>','</span>).<span class="hljs-title function_">forEach</span>(<span class=hljs-function><span class=hljs-params>cookie</span> =&gt;</span> {
      <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> [fullCookie] = cookie.<span class="hljs-title function_">trim</span>().<span class="hljs-title function_">split</span>(<span class=hljs-string>';'</span>)
      <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> [name, value] = fullCookie.<span class="hljs-title function_">split</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'='</span>)
      <span class=hljs-keyword>if</span> (name &amp;&amp; value) {
        cookieMap.<span class="hljs-title function_">set</span>(name.<span class="hljs-title function_">trim</span>(), value.<span class="hljs-title function_">trim</span>())
      }
    })
  }

  <span class="hljs-title function_">parseCookies</span>(cookies1)
  <span class="hljs-title function_">parseCookies</span>(cookies2)

  <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Array</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">from</span>(cookieMap.<span class="hljs-title function_">entries</span>()).<span class="hljs-title function_">map</span>(<span class=hljs-function>(<span class=hljs-params>[name, value]</span>) =&gt;</span> <span class=hljs-string>`<span class=hljs-subst>${name}</span>=<span class=hljs-subst>${value}</span>`</span>).<span class="hljs-title function_">join</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'; '</span>)
}

<span class=hljs-keyword>async</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">sendTelegramMessage</span>(<span class=hljs-params>message</span>) {
  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> telegramConfig = <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">parse</span>(<span class="hljs-variable constant_">TELEGRAM_JSON</span>)
  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> { telegramBotToken, telegramBotUserId } = telegramConfig
  <span class=hljs-keyword>const</span> url = <span class=hljs-string>`https://api.telegram.org/bot<span class=hljs-subst>${telegramBotToken}</span>/sendMessage`</span>
  
  <span class=hljs-keyword>try</span> {
    <span class=hljs-keyword>await</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">fetch</span>(url, {
      <span class=hljs-attr>method</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'POST'</span>,
      <span class=hljs-attr>headers</span>: { <span class=hljs-string>'Content-Type'</span>: <span class=hljs-string>'application/json'</span> },
      <span class=hljs-attr>body</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>({
        <span class=hljs-attr>chat_id</span>: telegramBotUserId,
        <span class=hljs-attr>text</span>: message
      })
    })
  } <span class=hljs-keyword>catch</span> (error) {
    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">error</span>(<span class=hljs-string>'Error sending Telegram message:'</span>, error)
  }
}

<span class=hljs-keyword>function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">delay</span>(<span class=hljs-params>ms</span>) {
  <span class=hljs-keyword>return</span> <span class=hljs-keyword>new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Promise</span>(<span class=hljs-function><span class=hljs-params>resolve</span> =&gt;</span> <span class=hljs-built_in>setTimeout</span>(resolve, ms))
}
